        <h2>Storyline</h2>
        
        <div class="inline canwrap">
            <p>
                <span>    Rachel Green, Ross Geller, Monica Geller, Joey Tribbiani, Chandler Bing and Phoebe Buffay are six 20 something year-olds, living off of one another in the heart of New York City. Over the course of ten years, this average group of buddies goes through massive mayhem, family trouble, past and future romances, fights, laughs, tears and surprises as they learn what it really means to be a friend.</span>
            </p>
        </div>

    <div id="titleDidYouKnow" class="article">
    <span class=rightcornerlink >
            <a href="/register/login?why=edit&ref_=tt_trv_trv"
rel="login">Edit</a>
    </span>
        <h2>Did You Know?</h2>
    <div id="trivia" class="txt-block">
        <h4>Trivia</h4>
    Joey's (<a href="/name/nm0001455?ref_=tt_trv_trv">Matt LeBlanc</a>'s) statue of a white dog was originally given to <a href="/name/nm0000098?ref_=tt_trv_trv">Jennifer Aniston</a> as a good luck present from her best friend when she started acting. She offered to lend it to the show for the episode where Joey became rich and bought a lot of stuff. After that episode, the producers decided to keep it.        <a href="trivia?ref_=tt_trv_trv"
class="nobr" >See more</a>  &raquo;
    </div>
                <hr />
     <div id="goofs"  class="txt-block">
        <h4>Goofs</h4>
Ross&#39; birthday changes several times during the show. In the 1x04, he mentions his birthday being 7 months before October 20th, which would be sometime in March (Pisces/Aries. Soon after he mentions his birthday being in December (Sagittarius/Capricorn), then discloses his birthday is precisely October 18th (Libra) in the later episodes.        <a href="trivia?tab=gf&ref_=tt_trv_gf"
class="nobr" >See more</a>  &raquo;
    </div>   
                <hr />
    <div id="quotes" class="text-block">
        <h4>Quotes</h4>
[<span class="fine">Chandler's roommate, Eddie has just accused him of sleeping with his ex girlfriend and killing his fish</span>]
<br /><a href="/name/nm0001435/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"
><span class="character">Phoebe</span></a>:
Why would you kill his fish?
<br /><a href="/name/nm0001612/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"
><span class="character">Chandler</span></a>:
Because, Phoebe, sometimes after you sleep with someone you have to kill a fish.
<br />        <a href="trivia?tab=qt&ref_=tt_trv_qu"
class="nobr" >See more</a> &raquo;
    </div>
                <hr />
     <div id="crazyCredits"  class="txt-block">
        <h4>Crazy Credits</h4>
    When the "The One That Could Have Been" was divided into two parts for syndication, a sequence was added that had the ending credits superimposed. It shows fat Monica dancing to some music while eating some food.  The original hourlong airing of "The One That Could Have Been" did not have the credits at the end of the first half hour and this scene was not involved.        <a href="trivia?tab=cz&ref_=tt_trv_cc"
class="nobr" >See more</a>  &raquo;
    </div>   
                <hr />
     <div id="alternateVersions"  class="txt-block">
        <h4>Alternate Versions</h4>
The episode &quot;The One Where Rachel Tells...&quot; originally featured Chandler making a joke about bombs at the airport on their honeymoon and was due to air soon after the events of 11 September 2001. The episode was rewritten, but the original scene is included on the Region 2 DVD.        <a href="alternateversions?tab=cz&ref_=tt_trv_alt"
class="nobr" >See more</a>  &raquo;
    </div>   
                <hr />
    <div id="connections" class="text-block">
        <h4>Connections</h4>

        <a href="trivia?tab=mc&ref_=tt_trv_cnn"
class="nobr" >See more</a> &raquo;
    </div>
